.如果真 (并且 (小于或等于 (到数值 (回补数量), 0), 小于或等于 (到数值 (回补金重), 0)))
    返回 (真)
.如果真结束
.如果真 (等于 (库房id, “”))
    赋值 (库房id, 全局_账户分组id)
.如果真结束

.如果 (等于 (库存存在行数, 0))
    增加记录 (全_MySQL写入, “xipunum_erp_shop_kucun”, 相加 (“poduct_code='”, 商品编码, “',”, “quantity='”, 回补数量, “',”, “jinzhong='”, 回补金重, “',”, “kufang='”, 库房id, “'”))
.否则
    执行SQL语句 (全_MySQL写入, 相加 (“UPDATE xipunum_erp_shop_kucun SET quantity = quantity + '”, 回补数量, “',jinzhong = jinzhong + '”, 回补金重, “' WHERE poduct_code = '”, 商品编码, “' AND kufang='”, 库房id, “'”))
.如果结束

执行SQL语句 (全_MySQL读取, 相加 (“SELECT a.id AS xiaoshouid,a.poduct_code AS outbound_product_code,b.product_name AS shop_product_name,b.item_number AS shop_item_number,c.title AS specification_title,b.caizhi AS material,b.quandu AS purity,MAX(d.company_condition) AS store_company_condition,b.single AS unit_weight,a.net_weight AS shop_gold_weight,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE(CASE WHEN b.quantity = 0 THEN a.net_weight ELSE b.weight / b.quantity * a.quantity END,a.net_weight),3) AS DECIMAL (20,3)) AS outbound_net_weight,a.basic_cost AS basic_cost,a.premium_cost AS apremium_cost,MAX(d.company_surcharge) AS store_company_surcharge,f.quantity AS shop_quantity,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE(f.jinzhong,0),3) AS DECIMAL (20,3)) AS kucunjin,a.xiaodan_amount AS xiaodan_amount,a.xiao_amount AS xiao_amount,a.quantity AS outbound_quantity,MAX(d.sales_surcharge) AS store_sales_surcharge,a.gold_price AS agold_price,a.sales_cost AS asales_cost,a.sales_surcharge AS asales_surcharge,a.zhekou AS discount,a.settlement AS settlement,a.shopping_guide AS ashopping_guide,g.name as gname FROM xipunum_erp_outbound AS a INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_shop AS b ON b.poduct_code = a.poduct_code LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_specs AS c ON c.id = b.specification_id INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_store AS d ON d.poduct_code = a.poduct_code LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_shop_kucun AS f ON f.poduct_code = a.poduct_code AND f.kufang = a.kufang LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_user AS g ON g.user = a.shopping_guide WHERE a.order_id = '”, 局部_销售单据id, “' GROUP BY a.id, a.poduct_code, b.product_name, b.item_number, c.title, b.caizhi, b.quandu, b.single, a.net_weight, a.basic_cost, a.premium_cost, a.xiaodan_amount, a.xiao_amount, a.quantity, a.gold_price, a.sales_cost, a.sales_surcharge, a.zhekou, a.settlement, c.shuliang, b.weight, b.quantity, f.quantity, f.jinzhong ORDER BY a.id ASC”))

    赋值 (销售工厂集句柄, 取记录集 (全_MySQL读取))
    赋值 (销售工厂数量, 取记录集行数 (销售工厂集句柄))
    .如果真 (大于 (销售工厂数量, 0))
        .计次循环首 (销售工厂数量, 销售工厂计次)
            赋值 (销售工厂名称, “”)
            读字段值 (销售工厂集句柄, “xsfactory”, 销售工厂名称)
            窗口_商品销售编辑.组合框销售工厂.加入项目 (到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (销售工厂名称), #编码_UTF_8, #编码_GBK, )), 销售工厂计次)
            到下一行 (销售工厂集句柄)
        .计次循环尾 ()
    .如果真结束
    释放记录集 (销售工厂集句柄)
.如果真结束
